# Parity Gaps — ranked by gameplay impact

_Generated 2026-06-25. 904 features with gaps, highest-impact first._

Score weights logic & liveness highest, then values/timing, then presentation/audio, scaled by category (core gameplay > niche entities). Intended divergences excluded.

| # | score | unit | feature | worst | gaps |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | 21.0 | `nexball` | `nexball.weapon.ballstealer` | logic:missing | WEP_NEXBALL / BallStealer weapon does not exist; there is no way to SHOOT or pass the carried ball.; No primary launch, no secondary tackle projectile (W_Nexball_Touch ball-steal), no homing safe-pass (W_Nexball_Think).; No weapon-arena handler, so Nexball is not enforced as a weapon-arena mode (carriers keep their normal weapons). |
| 2 | 21.0 | `onslaught` | `onslaught.captureshield` | logic:missing | No physical capture-shield entity around shielded generators/control points: an enemy player walks into a shielded node with no push-back, no GENERATOR/CONTROLPOINT_SHIELDED center notification on contact, and no spinning additive shield model. (The damage-ignore IS enforced via node.Shielded, and the weapon-damage blocked-by-shield SOUND hint IS played in IconDamage/GeneratorDamage; only the touch-push shield ENTITY + its center-print are missing.) |
| 3 | 21.0 | `onslaught` | `onslaught.spawn.teleport_choose` | logic:missing | No control-point-to-control-point teleport (use key / click-radar), no respawn-at-chosen-CP, no spawn_at_controlpoints / spawn_at_generator placement near owned nodes. Players spawn only via the generic team spawn system. The ons_spawn client command + clickradar HUD are absent. (spawn_choose defaults ON in Base.) ONS_TELEPORT/ONS_TELEPORT_ANTISPAM notifications registered as data but never emitted. |
| 4 | 21.0 | `onslaught` | `onslaught.presentation.csqc` | logic:missing | No generator/control-point/icon world models on the client; no progressive damage-model swaps; no icon bob/spin/punch-on-hit animation; no generator damage `frame`; no radar link lines; no objective death-cam (ENT_ONSCAMERA/WantEventchase/ons_camSetup) on round loss; no generator explosion sequence (rays/shockwave/gibs/electricity); no particle effects (EFFECT_SPARKS/CAP/RAGE/ROCKET_EXPLODE) or waypoint-sprite build/health bars. |
| 5 | 21.0 | `onslaught` | `onslaught.gen.unshielded_alarm` | logic:missing | ons_GeneratorThink (sv_onslaught.qc:1021) is NOT ported: while a generator is alive but UN-shielded (an enemy controls a linked CP), Base re-warns every 5s — the owning team gets CENTER_ONS_NOTSHIELDED_TEAM + the ONS_GENERATOR_ALARM siren (ATTEN_NONE), and the enemy team gets APP_TEAM_NUM(team, CENTER_ONS_NOTSHIELDED). The port wires no generator think entity (SpawnGenerator sets no Think), so this recurring 'your generator is exposed!' alarm never plays. The notifications (ONS_NOTSHIELDED_TEAM / _RED / _BLUE / _YELLOW / _PINK) and sound (ONS_GENERATOR_ALARM) are registered as data only. |

The barrel never visibly/audibly smokes or jams. UNCHANGED by Wave-1/2. |
| 7 | 19.5 | `clanarena` | `clanarena.join.late_join_observer` | logic:missing | While !allowed_to_spawn, QC forces a joining player to Observer (TRANSMUTE), sets INGAME_STATUS_JOINING, and sends INFO_CA_JOIN_LATE so they play from the next round. The port still has no INGAME_JOINING state and no allowed_to_spawn spawn gate, so mid-round joiners are not handled the QC way.; QC Bot_FixCount counts in-game-joined clients (so bots fill mid-round) -- not ported. |

| 16 | 18.75 | `weapon-tuba` | `weapon-tuba.audio.note_sound` | values:missing | NoteSample builds the correct per-pitch/instrument asset NAME (closing the baseline's flat 'tuba_loopnote.wav' which existed for NO file), but it looks up the RAW GetNote note with no cl_tuba_pitchstep rounding. The on-disk samples exist ONLY at multiples of 6 (-18,-12,-6,0,6,12,18,24); GetNote's common outputs (2,3,4,5,1,7,9,10,11,-1,-5,-4) have NO matching file, so the majority of played notes still resolve to a missing asset (likely silent). Only note 0 / +-6 (and the rare +-12/etc) hit a real sample.; No pitch-step crossfade / sound7 speed shift: Base picks the nearest available multiple-of-step sample and pitch-shifts the remainder; the port plays only the exact-name sample or nothing.; No sustained note: the port fires one static one-shot per blast tick (~0.05s) rather than a held loop that fades on release (cl_tuba_fadetime).; No client volume/attenuation cvars, no per-listener distance attenuation, no ENT_CLIENT_TUBANOTE networking (remote players' tuba notes are not driven by a dedicated note entity). |
